The example continues with update (using retry.RetryOnConflict to handle conflicts), list, and delete operations. This README explains the four fundamental operations: (1) Create a 2-replica Deployment with a selector matching pod labels, (2) Update the Deployment by modifying the replica count and container image using the retry pattern to handle conflicts, (3) List Deployments in a namespace, and (4) Delete the Deployment with foreground propagation policy.
